 </P> <P STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:0.5pt"><FONT COLOR="#FFFFFF">Stockholder Meeting Notice Tesla, Inc.&#146;s Annual Meeting of Stockholders will be held on Tuesday, June&nbsp;6, 2017 at 2:30 p.m. PDT
at Computer History Museum, 1401 N. Shoreline Blvd., Mountain View, CA 94043 Proposals to be voted on at the meeting are listed below along with the Board of Directors&#146; recommendations. The Board of Directors recommends a vote FOR all nominees,
FOR Proposal 2, every 3 YRS for Proposal 3, FOR Proposal 4, and AGAINST Proposal 5. 1. To elect three Class&nbsp;I directors to serve for a term of three years or until their respective successors are duly elected and qualified. Nominees:
01&#151;Elon Musk, 02&#151;Robyn M. Denholm, 03&#151;Stephen T. Jurvetson 2. A <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-binding</FONT> advisory vote on the approval of executive compensation. 3. A <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-binding</FONT>
advisory vote on the frequency of executive compensation votes. 4. To ratify the appointment of PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP as Tesla&#146;s independent registered public accounting firm for the fiscal year ending December&nbsp;31, 2017. 5. A
stockholder proposal regarding declassification of the Board of Directors. PLEASE NOTE &#150; YOU CANNOT VOTE BY RETURNING THIS NOTICE. To vote your shares you must vote online or request a paper copy of the proxy materials to receive a proxy card.
If you wish to attend and vote at the meeting, please bring this notice with you. Directions to Tesla, Inc.&#146;s 2017 Annual Meeting From San Jose via <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">US-101</FONT> North From East Bay via <FONT
